  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
  fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
  sharpObject - object
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
  (holdsAny ?a - agent)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (heatable ?o - object)
  (isHot ?o - object)
  (coolable ?o - object)
  (isCool ?o - object)
  (sliceable ?o - object)
  (isSliced ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number

 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?a ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (not (holdsAny ?a)))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holds ?a ?o) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (in ?o ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  agent
  receptacle
  object
  microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
  fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
  sharpObject - object
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
  (holdsAny ?a - agent)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (heatable ?o - object)
  (isHot ?o - object)
  (coolable ?o - object)
  (isCool ?o - object)
  (sliceable ?o - object)
  (isSliced ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?a ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (not (holdsAny ?a)))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holds ?a ?o) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (in ?o ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?o) (heatable ?o))
  :effect (and (isHot ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action CleanObject

  :effect (and (isClean ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action CoolObject

 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  agent
  receptacle
  object
  microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
  fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
  sharpObject - object
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
  (holdsAny ?a - agent)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (heatable ?o - object)
  (isHot ?o - object)
  (coolable ?o - object)
  (isCool ?o - object)
  (sliceable ?o - object)
  (isSliced ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?a ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (not (holdsAny ?a)))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holds ?a ?o) (holdsAny ?a) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holds ?a ?o)) (not (holdsAny ?a)) (in ?o ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  receptacle
  object
  microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
  fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
  sharpObject - object
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (heatable ?o - object)
  (isHot ?o - object)
  (coolable ?o - object)
  (isCool ?o - object)
  (sliceable ?o - object)
  (isSliced ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (heatable ?o))
  :effect (and (isHot ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (cleanable ?o))
  :effect (and (isClean ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (coolable ?o))
  :effect (and (isCool ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sliceable ?co))
  :effect (and (isSliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  receptacle
  object
  microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
  fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
  sharpObject - object
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (heatable ?o - object)
  (isHot ?o - object)
  (coolable ?o - object)
  (isCool ?o - object)
  (sliceable ?o - object)
  (isSliced ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (heatable ?o))
  :effect (and (isHot ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (cleanable ?o))
  :effect (and (isClean ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (coolable ?o))
  :effect (and (isCool ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action SliceObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sliceable ?co))
  :effect (and (isSliced ?co) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  receptacle
  object
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (cleanable ?o))
  :effect (and (isClean ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
)

 )

  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )

  (total-cost) - number
 )

  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)

  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  receptacle
  object
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (cleanable ?o))
  :effect (and (isClean ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  receptacle
  object
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (cleanable ?o))
  :effect (and (isClean ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  receptacle
  object
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (cleanable ?o))
  :effect (and (isClean ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  receptacle
  object
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
  microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
  fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
  sharpObject - object
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
  (isHeated ?o - object)
  (isCooled ?o - object)
  (isSliced ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CleanObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)

 )

  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
 )

  (at ?r - receptacle)

  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)

 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))

 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types
  receptacle
  object
  sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
  microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
  fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
  sharpObject - object
 )
 (:predicates
  (at ?r - receptacle)
  (opened ?r - receptacle)
  (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  (holding ?o - object)
  (handempty)
  (cleanable ?o - object)
  (isClean ?o - object)
  (toggleable ?o - object)
  (isOn ?o - object)
  (isHeated ?o - object)
  (isCooled ?o - object)
  (isSliced ?o - object)
  (isSharp ?o - object)
 )
 (:functions
  (total-cost) - number
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
  :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
  :precondition (at ?from)
  :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
  :effect (and (opened ?r) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CloseObject
  :parameters (?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (opened ?r) (handempty))
  :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action PutObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
  :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action UseObject
  :parameters (?o - object)
  :precondition (and (holding ?o) (toggleable ?o))
  :effect (and (when (isOn ?o) (not (isOn ?o))) (when (not (isOn ?o)) (isOn ?o)) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )

  :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o) (cleanable ?o))
  :effect (and (isClean ?o) (increase (total-cost) 5))
 )
 (:action HeatObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
  :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
  :effect (and (isHeated ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))
 )
 (:action CoolObject
  :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)

  :effect (and (isCooled ?o) (increase (total-cost) 1))

 )
